G\+S\+\_\+\+Aborted\+History writes aborted message to history metadata. 

Aborted\+History() writes an \char`\"{}\+Aborted\char`\"{} message to the history metadata, and updates the last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime metadata item. This works for any object with a \char`\"{}history\char`\"{} metadata item, and a \char`\"{}last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime\char`\"{} metadata item.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a7b6825b73fd902fa82581428da61334e}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ac06fa696ae73810823550a574fc9ffbc}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & I\+D of a file, an image, or any other valid object in a Geo\+Sci file.\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em history\+\_\+line} & This string is appended to the history metadata item for the given object, along with \char`\"{} $\ast$$\ast$$\ast$\+A\+B\+O\+R\+T\+E\+D$\ast$$\ast$$\ast$ \char`\"{}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Before writing to an image, write an aborted message in case of a run-\/time failure. After successfully modifying the image, write a new history, which over-\/writes the aborted message. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 bstring name = bfromcstr("/Image3");
3 image\_id=GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,name);
4 bdestroy(name);
5 
6 bstring tname = bfromcstr("Task\_name");
7 GS\_AbortedHistory(image\_id,tname);
8 bdestroy(tname);
9 
10      ... modify the image ....
11 
12 bstring tname2 = bfromcstr("Task\_name(task\_param1,task\_param2,...)");
13 GS\_AppendHistory(image\_id,tname2);
14 bassigncstr(tname2,"Task\_name: param1");
15 GS\_AppendHistory(file\_id,tname2);
16 bdestroy(tname2);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a7b6825b73fd902fa82581428da61334e}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History appends to the history metadata. 

Append\+History() appends the given string to the history metadata item, and updates the last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime metadata item. This works for any object with a \char`\"{}history\char`\"{} metadata item, and a \char`\"{}last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime\char`\"{} metadata item.

\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae74518625827cc1a4edc417eb54a59ca}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & I\+D of a file, an image, or any other valid object in a Geo\+Sci file. \\
\hline
 & {\em } & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ae74518625827cc1a4edc417eb54a59ca}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{object\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{metadata\+\_\+name, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ae74518625827cc1a4edc417eb54a59ca}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata appends the given string to the metadata item. 

\label{hdf5mine_8h_GS_AppendMetadata}%
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_AppendMetadata}{}%
\index{GS_AppendMetadata@{GS\+\_\+AppendMetadata}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aaf97760ec3c800c9e77adae19c54efc0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & I\+D of a file, and image, or any other valid object in a Geo\+Sci file. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em metadata\+\_\+name} & The name of the metadata item to update. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & This string is appended to the metadata item for the given object.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
After writing to an image, update it\textquotesingle{}s history. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 bstring name = bfromcstr("Image3");
3 image\_id=GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,name);
4 bdestroy(name);
5      ... modify the image ....
6 bstring history=bfromcstr("hsitory");
7 bstring history\_value = bfromcstr("Task\_name(task\_param1,task\_param2)");
8 GS\_AppendMetadata(image\_id,history,history\_value);
9 bdestroy(history);
10 bdestroy(history\_value);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
A special case is when writing a \char`\"{}history\char`\"{} metadata item. In this case, if the last line of the history contains \char`\"{}\+A\+B\+O\+R\+T\+E\+D\char`\"{}, we remove this last line, and append the new line. In essence this ends up \char`\"{}over-\/writing\char`\"{} the \char`\"{}\+A\+B\+O\+R\+T\+E\+D\char`\"{} line. The reason for this is to have an aborted message when there is a failure, but no aborted message on success. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a49ef49b18e11e59c0f7ffbd2968fb66d}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+File\+Existence@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+File\+Existence}}

4 \} else \{
5    printf("a.data does not exist\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}

\end{DoxyCode}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ac5aa76591622ce2842e104317f98f5ef}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Check\+Window\+Inside (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int $\ast$}]{window\+\_\+in, }
\item[{const int $\ast$}]{window\+\_\+enclosing}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ac5aa76591622ce2842e104317f98f5ef}


Check\+Window\+Inside checks if one Window is contained by another. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aad432d0513d576bfa0204514a58da96d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em window} & Vector containing desired window specification.~\newline
 window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} = Xoffset~\newline
 window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} = Yoffset~\newline
 window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} = Xsize~\newline
 window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} = Ysize~\newline
~\newline
 If window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is 0, window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} will be set to image X size -\/ window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}. ~\newline
 If window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} is 0, window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} will be set to image Y size -\/ window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em window\+\_\+enclosing} & Vector containing enclosing window specification. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E is returned is window is enclosed by window\+\_\+enclosing, False otherwise. Note that \char`\"{}enclosing\char`\"{} includes the case where any border are the same. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
In this example a user specified window is checked for validity within some other window. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1         ...
2 int dbiw[4];
3 int dbiw\_enclosing[4];
4         ...
5 // Determine user requested window.
6         ...
7 if( GS\_CheckWindowInside( dbiw, dbiw\_enclosing )) \{
8    printf("The window is enclosed.\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}
10         ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ab450cfcb4cec9d09153d63bd4cf5d697}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{datatype}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ab450cfcb4cec9d09153d63bd4cf5d697}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+From\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype returns the Geo\+Sci datatype for the given H\+D\+F datatype. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_adda18a93c5b245ba8848b73cc28add9b}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+To\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & A handle to an H\+D\+F5 datatype.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Geo\+Sci typecode is returned, and is 0 if invalid. Valid datatypes are\+:~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the Geo\+Sci equivalent of the H\+D\+F5 type H5\+T\+\_\+\+N\+A\+T\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T8\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 int gs\_type;
2 gs\_type = GS\_ConvertFromHDFDatatype(H5T\_NATIVE\_INT8);
3 if(!gs\_type) \{
4    printf("GS\_ConvertFromHDFDatatype failure\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Currently this checks against the H\+D\+F5 \char`\"{}\+N\+A\+T\+I\+V\+E\char`\"{} datatypes. I suspect this will not work if the data is in a different byte order. Need to fix this. (L\+E\+P\+: Aug 9, 2014). 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & An integer representing a Geo\+Sci datatype. Valid datatypes are\+:~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An H\+D\+F5 datatype is returned, and is negative if invalid. Complex datatypes should be H5\+Tclose()\textquotesingle{}d when done with them.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the H\+D\+F5 equivalent of the raster type complex-\/integer-\/16-\/bit. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t hdf\_type;
2 
3 hdf\_type = GS\_ConvertToHDFDatatype(GS\_DATATYPE\_CI16);
4 if(hdf\_type<0) \{
5    printf("GS\_ConvertToHDFDatatype failure\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Create\+Access\+Plist}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+Create\+Access\+Plist (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a34fb1b133fb3242cc26df4e106327527}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Create\+Access\+Plist creates an H\+D\+F5 access parameter list. 

The list that \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a34fb1b133fb3242cc26df4e106327527}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Create\+Access\+Plist()} returns is for use when creating or opening an H\+D\+F5 file. It sets raw data chunk cache parameters, as well as a driver for file I/\+O.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
This routine returns a valid H\+D\+F5 handle to an access\+\_\+plist, which can be used when creating or opening an H\+D\+F5 file.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
When creating a new file, we need to specify the access parameters. This routine returns an access list with \char`\"{}typical\char`\"{} parameters and parameter values set for most general uses. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t access\_plist;
2 access\_plist = GS\_CreateAccessPlist();
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline

6 \}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Copy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Copy (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Copy copies a dataset to an existing Group\+: this can be in the same group, a different group, or a different file. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em source} & A handle for a dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em destination\+\_\+group\+\_\+id} & The handle of the destination group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em destination\+\_\+dataset\+\_\+name} & The name of the new dataset to create.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The handle of the new dataset is returned. If it is less than zero, the copy failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Copy an image raster dataset to a new group, with a new name (\char`\"{}r3\char`\"{}). We have already opened the destination group. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t source\_raster\_id;
2 hid\_t destination\_group\_id;
3 hid\_t raster\_id;
4 bstring name = bfromcstr("r3");
5 raster\_id = GS\_DatasetCopy(source\_raster\_id, destination\_group\_id, name);
6 bdestroy(name);
7 if(raster\_id < 0) \{
8   printf("Failed to copy dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create creates a dataset in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em source} & A handle for the file or other container within which to create the dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The name of the dataset to create. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & The datatype of the numbers to store. Must be one of\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ndims} & The number of dimensions for the dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em size} & The (initial) size for each dimension \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em is\+\_\+extendable} & Set to T\+R\+U\+E to make the dataset size extendable, set to F\+A\+L\+S\+E to make the dataset size fixed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em is\+\_\+compressed} & Set to T\+R\+U\+E to make the dataset compressed, set to F\+A\+L\+S\+E to make the dataset uncompressed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The handle of the newly-\/created and opened dataset is returned. If it is less than zero, the creation failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Create an image raster dataset, with size 1024\+X512\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id, raster\_id;
2 int   size[2];
3 size[0]=512;
4 size[1]=1024;
5 bstring name = bfromcstr("r1");
6 raster\_id = GS\_DatasetCreate(image\_id, name,2,size,FALSE,FALSE);
7 bdestroy(name);
8 if(raster\_id < 0) \{
9   printf("Failed to create dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
10 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Bounds returns the rectangular bounding coordinates. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a6da4fa0d563fa782250970c9c6a31995}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for a dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em xmin} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em xmax} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ymin} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ymax} & The coordinates are returned with units that are consistent with the projection that is used. Typically the units are decimal degrees or meters.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} if there are any errors.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the bounds for a particular dataset\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t dataset\_id;
2 double xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax;
3 if(GS\_DatasetGetBounds(dataset\_id, &xmin, &xmax, &ymin, &ymax))\{
4   printf("X-range: %lf to %lf, Y-range: %lf to %lf\(\backslash\)n", xmin,xmax, ymin,ymax);
5 \} else \{
6   printf("no bounds\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}bounds\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the bounds that go with the data in this group. If this metadata does not exist, or there is an error in obtaining it or parsing it, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} is returned. Otherwise, the correct numbers are filled in, and {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Geo\+Sci datatype code is returned, and is 0 if there is an error. Valid datatypes are\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline

\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ab716d2f8b84a1db410259b81aaae6e1b}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ab716d2f8b84a1db410259b81aaae6e1b}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datum returns a description of the relevant datum if one exists. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for a dataset.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string describing the datum that is used for the data in this dataset. \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned if the datum cannot be determined, or on any other error. This string should be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when finished with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the datum for a particular dataset\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t dataset\_id;
2 bstring datum;
3 datum = GS\_DatasetGetDatum(dataset\_id);
4 printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(datum));
5 bdestroy(datum);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}spatialref\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the datum that is being used. If the spatialref metadata item does not exist, then \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned. If the spatialref metadata item exists, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+D\+A\+T\+U\+M\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is not found, then \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned, otherwise the string that follows this keyword is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a33c1f079f9c8912cdb50b255d9ce0d66}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{name, }
\item[{long int $\ast$$\ast$}]{size}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a33c1f079f9c8912cdb50b255d9ce0d66}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions returns the current dimensions for the Dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aceeb9596f55ad32a66123ac887c2c434}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datatype()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae0ffd3948a97404443965314444851a0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & File handle of selected Geo\+Sci file, or object handle of the container for the Dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & Name of object to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em size} & A vector of long integers\+: the size of each dimension\+: the number of data-\/objects per dimension.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of dimensions in the Dataset, or zero if there is an error. Also returns the length of each dimension (number of data-\/objects), in the integer vector {\ttfamily size}. This vector is allocated by this function, and should be G\+Free()\textquotesingle{}d when done with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the size of an image raster Dataset. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 int ndims;
3 long int *size;
4 bstring name = bfromcstr("r1");
5 ndims = GS\_DatasetGetDimensions(image\_id,name,&size);
6 bdestroy(name);
7 if(!ndims) \{
8    printf("GS\_DatasetGetDimensions failure\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}
10 printf("the dataset has %d dimensions:\(\backslash\)n",ndims);
11 for(i=0;i<ndims;i++) 
12   printf("dimension %d size is: %d data-objects\(\backslash\)n",i+1,size[i]);
13 GFree(size);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Note that this function returns dimensions in terms of the number of data-\/objects. It does N\+O\+T return the size in bytes. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a3be8ab589e38cd720f6d4bb2278b749e}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{long int $\ast$$\ast$}]{size}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a3be8ab589e38cd720f6d4bb2278b749e}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions\+By\+I\+D returns the current dimensions for the Dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a33c1f079f9c8912cdb50b255d9ce0d66}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Dimensions()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aceeb9596f55ad32a66123ac887c2c434}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Datatype()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae0ffd3948a97404443965314444851a0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & object handle of the Dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em size} & A vector of long integers\+: the size of each dimension\+: the number of data-\/objects per dimension.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of dimensions in the Dataset, or zero if there is an error. Also returns the length of each dimension (number of data-\/objects), in the integer vector {\ttfamily size}. This vector is allocated by this function, and should be G\+Free()\textquotesingle{}d when done with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the size of an image raster Dataset. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t raster\_id;
2 int ndims;
3 long int *size;
4 ndims = GS\_DatasetGetDimensionsByID(raster\_id,&size);
5 if(!ndims) \{
6    printf("GS\_DatasetGetDimensionsByID failure\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
8 printf("the dataset has %d dimensions:\(\backslash\)n",ndims);
9 for(i=0;i<ndims;i++) 
10   printf("dimension %d size is: %ld data-objects\(\backslash\)n",i+1,size[i]);
11 GFree(size);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Note that this function returns dimensions in terms of the number of data-\/objects. It does N\+O\+T return the size in bytes. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a6da4fa0d563fa782250970c9c6a31995}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a6da4fa0d563fa782250970c9c6a31995}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Projection returns a description of the relevant projection. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for a dataset.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string describing the projection that is used for the data in this dataset. \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned if the projection cannot be determined, or on any other error. This string should be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when finished with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the projection for a particular dataset\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t dataset\_id;
2 bstring projection;
3 projection = GS\_DatasetGetProjection(dataset\_id);
4 printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(projection));
5 bdestroy(projection);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}spatialref\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the projection that is being used. If the spatialref metadata item does not exist, then \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned. If the spatialref metadata item exists, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+P\+R\+O\+J\+C\+S\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is found, the string that follows this keyword is returned. If it is not found, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+G\+E\+O\+G\+C\+S\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is found, then the string \char`\"{}\+Geographic\char`\"{} is returned, otherwise the string \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a91429cf8a83c64b406f9312aaf561e4c}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Type}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Get\+Type returns the type of a Geo\+Sci Dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae0ffd3948a97404443965314444851a0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for the dataset.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The dataset type code is returned on success\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E} (10)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+A\+S\+T\+E\+R} (9)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T} (12)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E} (13)~\newline
~\newline
 On failure, the following type code is returned\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N} (0)
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the type of an image raster dataset\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t raster\_id;
2 
3 if(GS\_DatasetGetType(raster\_id) != GS\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_RASTER ) \{
4   printf("Dataset is not a raster.\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a78ec4d9837e5c2fb18d2f5df73e35976}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id, }
\item[{const long int $\ast$}]{offsets, }
\item[{const long int $\ast$}]{sizes, }
\item[{int}]{datatype, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{buffer}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a78ec4d9837e5c2fb18d2f5df73e35976}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read reads data from a dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae4294019ff956c155bb3840107b0b2ea}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae0ffd3948a97404443965314444851a0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & A handle for the dataset. Perhaps from \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em offsets} & Must supply an offset to the first data element to read for each dimension. Zero offset is used for reading starting with the first data-\/element. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sizes} & Must supply how many data elements to read for each dimension. Zero offset is used for reading starting with the first data-\/element. Using the offset and size for each dimension allows the specification of rectangular windows in n-\/dimensional space. For example, in 2-\/dimensions the window is\+:~\newline
 xoffset = offset\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, yoffset= offset\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}~\newline
 xsize = sizes\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, ysize = sizes\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & The datatype of the buffer. All the data that is read is converted to this datatype, and then returned to the caller in {\ttfamily buffer}. See the Details section for how this conversion is done. The valid datatypes are\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em buffer} & This is a pointer to enough memory to hold the data that is being read.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on sucess, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
We have a 2\+D dataset named \char`\"{}d4\char`\"{}, Read in from data elements 0 to 500 in dimension 1, and from data elements 100 to 700 in dimension 2. The data is stored as integers, but we\textquotesingle{}d like to read them as doubles. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 hid\_t dataset\_id;
3 double buffer[500*600];
4 int offsets[10], sizes[10];
5 bstring name = bfromcstr("d4");
6 dataset\_id = GS\_DatasetOpen(group\_id,name);
7 if(dataset\_id < 0)\{
8   printf("Failed to open dataset\(\backslash\)n");
9   bdestroy(name);
10   return;
11 \}
12 bdestroy(name);
13 offsets[0]=0;
14 offsets[1]=100;
15 sizes[0]=500;
16 sizes[1]=600;
17 if(!GS\_DatasetRead(dataset\_id, offsets, sizes, 
18                    GS\_DATATYPE\_R64, (void *)buffer)) \{
19   printf("Failed to read from dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
20 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Y\+E\+T\+: data type conversions....~\newline
 Y\+E\+T\+: deal with interleaving spec.....~\newline
 Y\+E\+T\+: indexing... 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Rename renames a dataset in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for the container of the dataset. This should be a group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em oldname} & Current name of dataset to rename. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em newname} & Desired new name of the dataset.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on sucess, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Rename a dataset from \char`\"{}r1\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}r4\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 bstring oldname = bfromcstr("r1");
3 bstring newname = bfromcstr("r2");
4 if(!GS\_GS\_DatasetRename(group\_id, oldname, newname) ) \{
5   printf("Failed to rename the dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
7 bdestroy(oldname);
8 bdestroy(newname);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a05bd3bd840dacdb60e9d456c8dec054e}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a05bd3bd840dacdb60e9d456c8dec054e}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Report returns a brief description of the dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a0e45ff4ddce2aa6a3b9bfc2fed6db732}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for a dataset.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string that provides a brief overview of the dataset. The string is zero-\/length on any error. Always bdestroy() the string when done with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get a report string on an image raster dataset. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t raster\_id;
2 bstring the\_report;
3 the\_report = GS\_DatasetReport(raster\_id);
4 printf("Report for the dataset: %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(the\_report));
5 bdestroy(the\_report);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
For an image raster, the report string looks like the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 [Raster] Landsat-Washita-SMEX3: Channel02; UINT8, 1024 X 4096
2 WGS84, UTM16T, X-Range: 274716.95 to 275716.95, Y-Range: 4684434.95 to 4684534.95
\end{DoxyCode}
 or more generally\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 [dataset-type] name: descriptor; datatype, dx X dy
2 Datum, Projection, Bounds
\end{DoxyCode}
 where the first string is the type of dataset, which, besides \char`\"{}\+Raster\char`\"{}, could include\+: \char`\"{}\+Internal File\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+Metadata\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+Metadata/\+Internal-\/\+File\char`\"{}, or \char`\"{}\+Unknown\char`\"{}. The second string is the name of the Dataset, while the third is the descriptor. The next one is the datatype. See \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aa4771ad431f7e00869566ecdb2b2520b}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String()} for a list of possible datatypes. The last string is the dimensions of the raster\+: dx X dy. For non-\/image rasters, the dimensions are 1-\/deminsional, and there are no Datum, Projection, or Bounds entries. N\+O\+T\+E\+: so far this only works for Image Rasters. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a0a4deab12ab7dfe07397b53270082fa6}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id, }
\item[{int}]{typecode}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a0a4deab12ab7dfe07397b53270082fa6}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Set\+Type set the type of a dataset in a Geo\+Sci file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dataset\+\_\+id} & A handle for the dataset. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em typecode} & An integer type code specifying the type of dataset. One of\+:~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E 10~\newline
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+A\+S\+T\+E\+R 9~\newline
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T 12~\newline
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E 13~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on sucess, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Set the type of an image raster dataset\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t raster\_id;
2 if(!GS\_DatasetSetType(raster\_id, GS\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_RASTER) ) \{
3   printf("Failed to set the type of the dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
4   return;
5 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ae4294019ff956c155bb3840107b0b2ea}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id, }
\item[{const long int $\ast$}]{offsets, }
\item[{const long int $\ast$}]{sizes, }
\item[{int}]{datatype, }
\item[{const void $\ast$}]{buffer}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ae4294019ff956c155bb3840107b0b2ea}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Write writes data to a dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a78ec4d9837e5c2fb18d2f5df73e35976}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Read()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae0ffd3948a97404443965314444851a0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & A handle for the dataset. Perhaps from \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aee86e45ef56ab3672a06a8358ceddd22}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dataset\+Open()}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em offsets} & Must supply an offset to the first data element to write for each dimension. Zero offset is used for writing starting with the first data-\/element. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sizes} & Must supply how many data elements to write for each dimension. Zero offset is used for writing starting with the first data-\/element. Using the offset and size for each dimension allows the specification of rectangular windows in n-\/dimensional space. For example, in 2-\/dimensions the window is\+:~\newline
 xoffset = offset\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, yoffset= offset\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}~\newline
 xsize = sizes\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, ysize = sizes\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & The datatype of the buffer. All the data that is written is converted from this datatype, to the datatype used by the Dataset. See the Details section for how this conversion is done. The valid datatypes are\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} (Unsigned Integer, 1-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} (Unsigned Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} (Signed Integer, 8-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} (Complex Integer, 8-\/bit (not supported))~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} (Unsigned Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} (Signed Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} (Complex Integer, 16-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} (Unsigned Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} (Signed Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} (Complex Integer, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} (Complex Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} (Real, 32-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} (Real, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} (Complex, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} (Complex, 128-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} (Unsigned Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} (Signed Integer, 64-\/bit)~\newline
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em buffer} & This is a pointer to enough memory to hold the data that is being written.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on sucess, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
We have a 2\+D dataset named \char`\"{}d4\char`\"{}, Write to data elements 0 to 500 in dimension 1, and to data elements 100 to 700 in dimension 2. The data is stored in the Dataset as integers, and we are sending doubles, which therefore need to be converted. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 hid\_t dataset\_id;
3 double buffer[500*600];
4 int offsets[10], sizes[10];
5 dataset\_id = GS\_DatasetOpen(group\_id,"d4");
6 if(dataset\_id < 0)\{
7   printf("Failed to open dataset\(\backslash\)n");
8   return;
9 \}
10 offsets[0]=0;
11 offsets[1]=100;
12 sizes[0]=500;
13 sizes[1]=600;
14 if(!GS\_DatasetWrite(dataset\_id, offsets, sizes, 
15                    GS\_DATATYPE\_R64, (void *)buffer)) \{
16   printf("Failed to write to dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
17 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Y\+E\+T\+: data type conversions....~\newline
 Y\+E\+T\+: deal with interleaving spec.....~\newline
 Y\+E\+T\+: indexing... 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_aa4771ad431f7e00869566ecdb2b2520b}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String (

)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aa4771ad431f7e00869566ecdb2b2520b}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+String return a string representing the datatype. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+As\+Integer(), G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+Numbytes()
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & An integer representing a Geo\+Sci datatype. Valid datatypes\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} 1 A single bit ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} 4 Complex 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} 5 Unsigned 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} 16 Unsigned 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 17 Signed 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The valid bstring is returned always. It has a non-\/zero length on success, zero length on failure. Need to bdestroy() it when done.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the datatype of a raster channel\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 int raster\_datatype;
2 bstring thetype = GS\_DatatypeAsString(raster\_datatype);
3 if(bstrlen(thetype)>0) \{
4    printf("The datatype is %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(thetype));
5 \} else \{
6    printf("The datatype is unknown.\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
8 bdestroy(thetype);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a06f9bc1db501d6aca19778e429b29e15}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+Is\+Complex@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+Is\+Complex}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Datatype\+Is\+Complex returns T\+R\+U\+E if a complex datatype.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & An integer representing a Geo\+Sci datatype. Valid datatypes\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} 1 A single bit ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} 4 Complex 8-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} 5 Unsigned 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} 16 Unsigned 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 17 Signed 64-\/bit integer ~\newline
 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned for complex datatypes, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} for others, and {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+O\+R} otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Determine if a datatype is complex\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 int datatype;
2 if(GS\_DatatypeIsComplex(datatype)==TRUE)\{
3    printf("the datatype is complex.\(\backslash\)n);
4 \} else \{
5    printf("the datatype is not complex\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 Note that if one does not compare with T\+R\+U\+E, but instead uses the default C behavior of anything not 0 being true\+: both T\+R\+U\+E and E\+R\+R\+O\+R are non-\/zero and so one may not get the expected behavior. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a8b558973d6ede1ec1c665ce6b067d5c4}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Dirname@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dirname}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Dirname}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}char$\ast$ G\+S\+\_\+\+Dirname (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a8b558973d6ede1ec1c665ce6b067d5c4}


Dirname returns the directory name for a U\+N\+I\+X pathname. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a30baf67ef893fad57fe691473bc26b33}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Create()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The name of an object in an existing Geo\+Sci file. Use Unix filenaming conventions, giving the full pathname, starting with \char`\"{}/\char`\"{}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A character string is returned with the directory part of the name which does not end in a \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}. G\+Free() it when done. If there are errors, a N\+U\+L\+L pointer is returned. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}
1 char *dir;
2 
3 dir = Dirname("/groupa/group1/image4");
4 if(!dir)\{
5   printf("Dirname failed\(\backslash\)n");
6   exit(-1);
7 \}
8 
9 ...use dir here....
10 
11 GFree(dir);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close (

)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close closes a Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & File handle for Geo\+Sci file to be closed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned on success, while {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} is returned on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
This example opens and then closes a standard Geo\+Sci file\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t   file\_id;
2 bstring filename = bfromcstr("testimage.hd5");
3 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
4 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen( filename, access );
5 bdestroy(filename);
6 bdestroy(access);
7   ... use the file ...
8 GS\_FileClose( file\_id );
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_abba9fbf0c3f0df085d9450411f214991}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close\+All\+Objects@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close\+All\+Objects}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Commit\+Datatypes commits the complex raster datatypes to a file. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & The file I\+D\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
After creating a new file, commit the complex raster datatypes to it\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 if(!GS\_FileCommitDatatypes(file\_id))\{
3    printf("failed to commit the complex raster datatypes to the file\(\backslash\)n");
4 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
H\+D\+F-\/5 requires user-\/created raster datatypes to be \char`\"{}committed\char`\"{} to a file where these datatypes are used. Since all the complex raster datatypes used in Geo\+Sci are \char`\"{}user-\/created\char`\"{}, we need to make sure that they are always committed. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a27f03abbbf414b471cbe4ef8ebf17813}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Copy@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Copy}}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{filename}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create creates an empty Geo\+Sci datafile. 

The basic file metadata is created, but nothing else. \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create()} assumes the file does N\+O\+T exist before creating it, and will return an error if a file with the same name already exists.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}, G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Georef\+I\+O()
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em filename} & Name of file to be created. If there is no \char`\"{}.\+hd5\char`\"{} extension, this routine will create a file with the \char`\"{}.\+hdf5\char`\"{} extension.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The routine returns a file handle on success, which is negative if creation fails.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Create an empty file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t       file\_id;
2 bstring     filename=bfromcstr("testimage.hd5");
3 file\_id = GS\_FileCreate( filename );
4     ... use the file ...
5 GS\_FileClose( file\_id );
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
For every Geo\+Sci file we create we also \char`\"{}commit\char`\"{} every complex datatype into it. That way, no matter what a user does, the datatypes are there for them to use. This simplifies the other codes, who now need not be concerned about dealing with this. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_af6756c2c0e953c726dc7aa04172b5543}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{descriptor}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_af6756c2c0e953c726dc7aa04172b5543}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata Creates metadata in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af6756c2c0e953c726dc7aa04172b5543}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Metadata()} creates a new metadata group to store per-\/file metadata in, it then fills them in with default values, and the file descriptor string that is passed in.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
File\+Create()
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & The file I\+D \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em descriptor} & A character string describing the file contents.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Create a new file named \char`\"{}av1.\+h5\char`\"{} and set it\textquotesingle{}s file metadata, in particular make the file descriptor string be \char`\"{}\+Aviris over Boston, M\+A\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 bstring filename = bfromcstr("av1.h5");
3 file\_id = GS\_FileCreateEmpty(filename);
4 bdestroy(filename);
5 if(file\_id > 0) \{
6    bstring description = bfromcstr("Aviris over Boston, MA");
7    if(GS\_FileCreateMetadata(file\_id,description)\{
8       printf("success\(\backslash\)n");
9    \}
10    bdestroy(description);
11 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
The file metadata is stored in a group named \char`\"{}/\+\_\+\+Header\char`\"{}. The file metadata items are\+: {\ttfamily grouptype} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+Metadata\char`\"{}}), {\ttfamily filetype} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+G\+E\+O\+S\+C\+I\char`\"{}}), {\ttfamily software\+\_\+version} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+V0.\+0.\+1\char`\"{}}), {\ttfamily creation\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily history}, and {\ttfamily descriptor}, the last one being set by a call to this function.

Note that until the file metadata is set up correctly the file is not recognized as a valid Geo\+Sci file, and so most functions in this library will not operate on it successfully. Because of this, the file creation function, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create}, calls this function as part of the file creation process. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a040861a90b5908480ad6a8d46ad0c9aa}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Delete@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Delete}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Delete@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Delete}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a8cd208fe090b959fe3142a3fc93cab14}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{object\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a8cd208fe090b959fe3142a3fc93cab14}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush forces the datafile to be updated. 

\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8cd208fe090b959fe3142a3fc93cab14}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Flush()} forces all changes to a file to be flushed to the hard drive, forcing them to occur rather than waiting in a \char`\"{}buffered\char`\"{} state.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & I\+D of a file, an image, or any other valid object in a Geo\+Sci datafile.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
After writing to an image, make sure all changes are written to disk. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 bstring image\_name=bfromcstr("Image3");
3 image\_id=GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,image\_name);
4 bdestroy(image\_name);
5      ... modify the image ....
6 GS\_FileFlush(image\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}
 Note that we could have used file\+\_\+id as well. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ac4f9a6f40f8d67b12bf70742f584ac70}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Open@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Open}}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_aff67a8e73595be937141f2823f90ad9e}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Writeable@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Writeable}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Writeable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Writeable (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aff67a8e73595be937141f2823f90ad9e}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Is\+Writeable returns if file is writeable or not. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af791d7b4eab9221cd18790afdb28013c}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Lock()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a61d32b1e9d78286b2da48a300ce44ab2}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Unlock()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & The handle of the file, or any object in the file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} if the file associated with the given handle is writeable, or {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} if not. Returns {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+O\+R} (-\/1) if cannot determine the status.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}
1 int status;
2          ...
3 status = GS\_FileIsWriteable(file\_id);
4 if(status < 0)\{
5   printf("Could not determine read/write status of file.\(\backslash\)n");
6   return;
7 \}
8 if(status==FALSE) return;
9 ...here we can write to the file....
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
A file is writeable if it was opened in read/write mode using G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open, and if the {\ttfamily writeable} metadata is {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E}, which can be changed via a call to G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Lock, and G\+S\+\_\+object\+Unlock. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open@{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{access}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}


G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open opens a Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dbname} & The name of the Geo\+Sci datafile to be opened. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em access} & Read/\+Write flag\+:~\newline
 \char`\"{}r\char`\"{} \+: Open file for Read only~\newline
 \char`\"{}r+\char`\"{}\+: Open file for Read/\+Write\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the {\ttfamily hid\+\_\+t} file handle for the file opened. If the Geo\+Sci file does not exist, a negative file handle is returned, and the global {\ttfamily error\+\_\+string} is set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Open a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{} for read/write. Note that the default extension \char`\"{}.\+hd5\char`\"{} is tried by \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()} if the file \char`\"{}testimage\char`\"{} does not exist. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t      file\_id;
2 bstring filename= bfromcstr("testimage");
3 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
4 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen ( filename, access);
5 bdestroy(filename);
6 bdestroy(access);
7   ... use the file ...
8 GS\_FileClose (file\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Rename renames an existing Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create\+Empty(), \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a27f03abbbf414b471cbe4ef8ebf17813}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Copy()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em oldname} & Name of existing file to rename. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em newname} & New name to be assigned to file \textquotesingle{}oldname\textquotesingle{}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Rename a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}sirc\+\_\+april.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring oldname = bfromcstr("testimage.hd5");
2 bstring newname = bfromcstr("sirc\_april.hd5");
3 if(!GS\_FileRename( oldname, newname ))\{
4     printf("GS\_FileRename failure.\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
6 bdestroy(oldname);
7 bdestroy(newname);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a10da9d7f59777a80a3aa6eb0fda3f3e0}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Rename()} will return an error if the file is open, or if a file with the same newname already exists. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Report summarizes the contents of a Geo\+Sci datafile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em filename} & Name of datafile to be queried. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em report\+\_\+string} & The returned report, as a multi-\/line string. On entry, must be a valid bstring.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure. The {\ttfamily report\+\_\+string} contains a multi-\/line string with contents like the following\+:~\newline
Filename\+: test123.\+h5 \mbox{[}R\+W\mbox{]}, Empty File~\newline
 Created\+: 19\+:37\+:45 23-\/\+Jun-\/2016 , Last Update\+: 19\+:37\+:45 23-\/\+Jun-\/2016~\newline
 image\+\_\+aa\+: \mbox{[}Image\mbox{]} S\+I\+R-\/\+C Raco 102.\+4 S\+R\+L-\/1
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Obtain report on a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring report\_string=bfromcstr("");
2 bstring filename = bfromcstr("testimage.hd5");
3 if(GS\_FileReport(filename,report\_string))\{
4    printf("%s",report\_string);
5 \} else \{
6    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",error\_string);
7 \}
8 bdestroy(filename);
9 bdestroy(report\_string);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & An integer representing a Geo\+Sci raster datatype. Valid datatypes\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} 1 A single bit~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} 4 Complex 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} 5 Unsigned 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point ~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} 16 Unsigned 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 17 Signed 64-\/bit integer~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The bstring is returned on success, or a zero-\/length bstring on failure. bdestroy() it when done. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyCode}

2 bassignstr(str,GS\_GetRasterTypeAsString(GS\_DATATYPE\_R64));

4 bdestroy(str);
\end{DoxyCode}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a99c937f579059c0ebea985ce6f61158f}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a99c937f579059c0ebea985ce6f61158f}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Get\+Valid\+File\+I\+D returns a valid File\+I\+D that contains the object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & An id for an object in a Geo\+Sci file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A valid File\+I\+D is returned or a value less than 0 on error.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Assume one has opened a file and an image, passes the image\+\_\+id into a function, and needs the file\+\_\+id asociated with the image\+\_\+id. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id, file\_id;
2 file\_id = GS\_GetValidFileID(image\_id);
3 if(file\_id < 0) \{
4    printf("Could not get valid file\_id\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This function either returns an {\ttfamily id} that is the same as the passed-\/in {\ttfamily id}, but with an incremented reference-\/count, or it returns a different {\ttfamily id}, also with an incremented reference-\/count. The user should always \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close()} this {\ttfamily id} when done with it. The associated file will only be closed when the reference count reaches zero.

A typical usage of this is to make sure a passed-\/in {\ttfamily id} is a {\ttfamily file\+\_\+id}. In such a case, this will increment the reference count by 1, and the user should then \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close()} it when done, which will N\+O\+T close the file that the passed-\/in {\ttfamily file\+\_\+id} refers to.

In another scenario, where the code needs to return a newly-\/opened object in the passed-\/in {\ttfamily file\+\_\+id}, one needs to be more careful. Do not use this routine. Instead call G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+File(id) to make sure the {\ttfamily id} refers to a file, and return an error if it doesn\textquotesingle{}t. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

4 bstring newname = bfromcstr("/Boston\_day3");

7   printf("Failed to copy group.\(\backslash\)n");
8 \}

\end{DoxyCode}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Create creates a new group in a Geo\+Sci Datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8176d399de52c42c01724e5ef829df4c}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & A handle for an already-\/open Geo\+Sci datafile. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em groupname} & The name of the group in an existing Geo\+Sci datafile to be created. Use Unix/\+Web filenaming conventions, giving the full pathname, starting with \char`\"{}/\char`\"{}. All but the last component of this name must already exist.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
A valid handle to the new group is returned on success. A negative value is returned on failure.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Create a group named \char`\"{}/group3\char`\"{} in an already-\/open Geo\+Sci file. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id, group\_id;
2 bstring groupname = bfromcstr("/group3");
3 group\_id = GS\_GroupCreate(file\_id,groupname);
4 bdestroy(groupname);
5 if(group\_id < 0 )\{
6   printf("GS\_GroupCreate failure\(\backslash\)n");
7   return;
8 \}
9 .... use it here ....
10 GS\_GroupClose(group\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a8176d399de52c42c01724e5ef829df4c}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete (
