)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a8176d399de52c42c01724e5ef829df4c}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Delete deletes a group in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & A handle for the already-\/open Geo\+Sci file. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+name} & The name of the group, starting with a \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} and giving the full path to the group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned if the group and all objects it contains are successfully deleted, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Delete an image group named Image1 (should normally call \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a869dadbfd60acbc69f13fd88f202d4cc}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Delete()})\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 bstring imagename=bfromcstr("/Image1");
3 if(!GS\_GroupDelete(file\_id, imagename))\{
4    printf("Failed to delete group\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
6 bdestroy(imagename);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
Deletes the group and all objects it contains. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a9f63935cd0326fb2105c2330d89ed176}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{group\+\_\+id, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{xmin, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{xmax, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{ymin, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{ymax}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a9f63935cd0326fb2105c2330d89ed176}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Bounds returns the rectangular bounding coordinates. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1a2d0ab9bb4c96f13b8e04aa1a4d3d63}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for a group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em xmin} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em xmax} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ymin} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ymax} & The coordinates are returned with units that are consistent with the projection that is used. Typically the units are decimal degrees or meters.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} if there are any errors.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the bounds for a particular group\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 double xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax;
3 if(GS\_GroupGetBounds(group\_id, &xmin, &xmax, &ymin, &ymax))\{
4   printf("X-range: %lf to %lf, Y-range: %lf to %lf\(\backslash\)n", xmin,xmax, ymin,ymax);
5 \} else \{
6   printf("no bounds\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}bounds\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the bounds that go with the data in this group. If this metadata does not exist, or there is an error in obtaining it or parsing it, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} is returned. Otherwise, the correct numbers are filled in, and {\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a0ca7131d7a70595c1e984e965c91c1fc}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{group\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a0ca7131d7a70595c1e984e965c91c1fc}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Datum returns a description of the relevant datum if one exists. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for a group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string describing the datum that is used for the data in this group. \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned if the datum cannot be determined, or on any other error. This string should be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when finished with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the datum for a particular group\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 bstring datum;
3 datum = GS\_GroupGetDatum(group\_id);
4 printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",datum);
5 bdestroy(datum);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}spatialref\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the datum that is being used. If the spatialref metadata item does not exist, then \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned. If the spatialref metadata item exists, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+D\+A\+T\+U\+M\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is not found, then \char`\"{}\+No Datum\char`\"{} is returned, otherwise the string that follows this keyword is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a1a2d0ab9bb4c96f13b8e04aa1a4d3d63}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{group\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a1a2d0ab9bb4c96f13b8e04aa1a4d3d63}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Projection returns a description of the relevant projection. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for a group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string describing the projection that is used for the data in this group. \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned if the projection cannot be determined, or on any other error. This string should be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when finished with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Print the projection for a particular group\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t group\_id;
2 bstring projection;
3 projection = GS\_GroupGetProjection(group\_id);
4 printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",projection);
5 bdestroy(projection);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This routine looks at the \char`\"{}spatialref\char`\"{} metadata string in order to determine the projection that is being used. If the spatialref metadata item does not exist, then \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned. If the spatialref metadata item exists, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+P\+R\+O\+J\+C\+S\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is found, the string that follows this keyword is returned. If it is not found, then the routine looks for the keyword \char`\"{}\+G\+E\+O\+G\+C\+S\char`\"{} which should appear in the W\+K\+T portion of this metadata. If it is found, then the string \char`\"{}\+Geographic\char`\"{} is returned, otherwise the string \char`\"{}\+No Projection\char`\"{} is returned. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a87f933403edd6b10b47f8bad5da81fa9}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Type}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Type}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a87f933403edd6b10b47f8bad5da81fa9}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Get\+Type returns the type of a group in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for the group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The dataset type code is returned on success\+:~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P} 1~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E} 2~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R} 3~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R2\+D} 4~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R3\+D} 5~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+N} 6~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H2\+D} 7~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H3\+D} 8~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+A\+S\+T\+E\+R} 9~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E} 10~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T} 12~\newline
{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E} 13~\newline
On failure, the following type code is returned\+: \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get the type of an image\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 if(GS\_GroupGetType(image\_id) != GS\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_IMAGE ) \{
3   printf("Dataset is not an image, as expected.\(\backslash\)n");
4 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open opens an existing group in a Geo\+Sci datafile.

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

1 hid\_t file\_id, meta\_id;
2 meta\_id = GS\_GroupOpen(file\_id, bsstatic("\_Header"));
3 if(meta\_id < 0) \{
4   printf("Failed to open group.\(\backslash\)n");
5 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Rename renames a group in a Geo\+Sci datafile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & A handle for the file, or other container of the group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em oldname} & Current name of group to rename. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em newname} & Desired new name of the group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on sucess, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Rename an image from \char`\"{}/\+S\+I\+R\+C-\/1\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}/\+S\+I\+R\+C-\/1a\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 bstring oldname = bfromcstr("/SIRC-1");
3 bstring newname = bfromcstr("/SIRC-1a");
4 if(!GS\_GS\_GroupRename(file\_id, oldname, newname) ) \{
5   printf("Failed to rename the group.\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
7 bdestroy(oldname);
8 bdestroy(newname);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Report@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Report}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Report}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Report (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{group\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aff77b4a7dd8f74adeae18efb6a331382}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Report returns a one-\/line brief description of the group. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab3f99f9287304ba4526a9fb04ee734fe}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Close()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8df2ff48d2ef0ffa139a42b996581af6}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Open()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & A handle for a group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string that provides a brief overview of the group. The string is zero-\/length on any error. Always bdestroy() the string when done with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Get a report string on an image. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t raster\_id;
2 bstring the\_report;
3 the\_report = GS\_GroupReport(raster\_id);
4 printf("Report for the dataset: %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(the\_report));
5 bdestroy(the\_report);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
For Metadata Groups, we use the following string\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 [Metadata][RW] name: descriptor; last-update-datetime
\end{DoxyCode}
 For Image Groups, we use the following string\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 [Image][RW] name: descriptor; last-update-datetime
\end{DoxyCode}
 For Vector Groups, we use the following string\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 [Vector][RW] name: descriptor; last-update-datetime
2 Datum, Projection, Upper-left Lat/long, Lower-right Lat/Long
\end{DoxyCode}
 Where \char`\"{}\+R\+W\char`\"{} stands for a group that is both Readable and Writeable, while \char`\"{}\+R\+O\char`\"{} would be used for a group that is Read-\/only. Other Group-\/types have yet to be defined. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a56462ec6cf3a1fdc77f63627c3462f5f}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Set\+Type@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Group\+Set\+Type}}

{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E} 2~\newline

G\+S\+\_\+\+G\+S\+Object\+Type\+As\+String returns printable version of the object type. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+type} & Object type. One of\+:~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P 1~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E 2~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R 3~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R2\+D 4~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R3\+D 5~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+N 6~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H2\+D 7~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H3\+D 8~\newline

 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T 12~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E 13 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
On success, the routine returns the string representation of the {\ttfamily object\+\_\+type} according to the following table\+:~\newline
 \begin{TabularC}{2}
\hline
\rowcolor{lightgray}{\bf object type }&{\bf returned string  }\\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P &Metadata \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E &Image \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R &Vector \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R2\+D &Vector2\+D \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R3\+D &Vector3\+D \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+N &T\+I\+N \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H2\+D &Mesh2\+D \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H3\+D &Mesh3\+D \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R\+A\+S\+T\+E\+R &Raster \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E &Internal File \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E &File \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T &Metadata Dataset \\\cline{1-2}
G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E &Metadata Internal File \\\cline{1-2}
\end{TabularC}
On failure, the string \char`\"{}\+Unknown Object Type\char`\"{} is returned.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Note that the returned string should N\+O\+T be G\+Free\textquotesingle{}d or bdestroy\textquotesingle{}d when done. \begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Obtain list of objects in a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1     ...
2 bstring *objnames;
3 int objtypes;
4 int nobjs;
5 int i;
6 
7 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen("testimage.hd5","r+");
8 if(file\_id<0)\{
9    printf("GS\_FileOpen failed\(\backslash\)n");
10    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
11    exit(-1);
12 \}//endif
13 
14 if(!GS\_ObjectGetGSChildren(file\_id, &nobjs, &objnames,&objtypes))\{
15    printf("GS\_ObjectGetGSChildren failed\(\backslash\)n");
16    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
17    exit(-1);
18 \}
19 
20 // print results:
21 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
22    printf("obj# %d: %s (%s)\(\backslash\)n",i,bdata(objnames[i]),
23            bdata(GS\_GSObjectTypeAsString(objtypes[i])));
24 \}
25 
26 // clean up:
27 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
28    bdestroy(objnames[i]);
29 \}
30 GFree(objnames);
31 GFree(objtypes);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+H5\+Object\+Type\+As\+String returns a printable version of H\+D\+F5 object type. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+type} & object type, as an integer. One of\+:~\newline
 H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P~\newline
 H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T~\newline
 H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+D\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
On success, the routine returns the string representation of the object type according to the following table\+:
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{TabularC}{2}
\hline
\rowcolor{lightgray}{\bf object type }&{\bf returned string  }\\\cline{1-2}
H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P &Group \\\cline{1-2}
H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+S\+E\+T &Dataset \\\cline{1-2}
H5\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+D\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E &Named Datatype \\\cline{1-2}
\end{TabularC}
On failure, the string \char`\"{}\+Unknown Object Type\char`\"{} is returned.

Note that the returned string should N\+O\+T be bdestroy\textquotesingle{}d when done. \begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Obtain list of objects in a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1     ...
2 char **objnames;
3 int objhdftypes;
4 int nobjs;
5 int i;
6 
7 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(bsstatic("testimage.hd5"),bsstatic("r+"));
8 if(file\_id<0)\{
9    printf("GS\_FileOpen failed\(\backslash\)n");
10    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
11    exit(-1);
12 \}//endif
13 
14 if(!GS\_ObjectGetH5Children(file\_id, &nobjs, &objnames,&objhdftypes))\{
15    printf("GS\_ObjectGetH5Children failed\(\backslash\)n");
16    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
17    exit(-1);
18 \}
19 
20 // print results:
21 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
22    printf("obj# %d: %s (%s)\(\backslash\)n",i,bdata(objnames[i]),
23            GS\_H5ObjectTypeAsString(objhdftypes[i]));
24 \}
25 
26 // clean up:
27 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
28    bdestroy(objnames[i]);
29 \}
30 GFree(objnames);
31 GFree(objhdftypes);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a1caf38d5d8079e8f27d872f90388f856}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype\+Close@{G\+S\+\_\+\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype\+Close}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype\+Close}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype\+Close (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a1caf38d5d8079e8f27d872f90388f856}


G\+S\+\_\+\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype\+Close closes an H\+D\+F datatype. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_adda18a93c5b245ba8848b73cc28add9b}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+To\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & The id of the datatype.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, E\+R\+R\+O\+R (-\/1) on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
After opening a datatype using \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_adda18a93c5b245ba8848b73cc28add9b}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Convert\+To\+H\+D\+F\+Datatype()}, close it\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t hdf\_type;
2 hdf\_type = GS\_ConvertToHDFDatatype(GS\_DATATYPE\_R64);
3 if(hdf\_type<0)\{
4    printf("GS\_ConvertToHDFDatatype failed\(\backslash\)n");
5    return;
6 \}
7 if(!GS\_HDFDatatypeClose(hdf\_type))\{
8   printf("failed to close the datatype\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This function is not needed for most types, as they are not really opened to begin with. However, the complex datatypes are opened, and so need to be closed. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a6aebc2231c887d1bec1f10e361e649d9}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}hid\+\_\+t G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{image\+\_\+name, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{image\+\_\+descriptor}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a6aebc2231c887d1bec1f10e361e649d9}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create creates a new image in a Geo\+Sci file and opens it. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_af07a914cd15aa25e3f6d92fe7ae005fa}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Create}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a895023bd9cb5070686c7bcd0159e2133}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em imagename} & Name of the image to create. Must not be the same as any other existing object in the file or the creation will fail. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+descriptor} & A string describing the contents of the image. This describes all the channels, in a general sense. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns an image handle on success, or a negative integer on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Create an image named \char`\"{}sirc-\/102.\+41-\/spring\char`\"{} with an image descriptor of \char`\"{}raw slc data\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1     ...
2 hid\_t       file\_id;
3 bstring name = bfromcstr("sirc-102.41-spring");
4 bstring descriptor = bfromcstr("raw slc data");
5 
6 image\_id = GS\_ImageCreate(file\_id, name, descriptor)
7 if(image\_id < 0) \{
8    printf("image creation failed.\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}// endif
10 bdestroy(name);
11 bdestroy(descriptor);
12     ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a76917af6500623493e7aa7a14b2aa2c7}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{image\+\_\+name, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{descriptor}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a76917af6500623493e7aa7a14b2aa2c7}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create\+Metadata fills the standard image metadata attributes with the values that are passed in. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a6aebc2231c887d1bec1f10e361e649d9}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & The file I\+D \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+name} & A character string giving the name of the image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em descriptor} & A character string describing the image contents.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
After creating a new image named \char`\"{}datatake 34\char`\"{} in a file named \char`\"{}av1.\+h5\char`\"{}, we must set the metadata for the image before the image object can be used. The descriptor is \char`\"{}\+Apr 3, 2012, 2\+:18 P\+M\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 bstring filename=bfromcstr("av1.h5");
3 bstring access=bfromcstr("r+");
4 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(filename,access);
5 bdestroy(filename);
6 bdestroy(access);
7 if(file\_id > 0) \{
8    ... create a group with datasets in it that represent the image...
9    bstring name = bfromcstr("datatake 34");
10    bstring descriptor = bfromcstr("Apr 3, 2012, 2:18 PM");
11    if(GS\_ImageCreateMetadata(file\_id,name,descriptor)\{
12       printf("success\(\backslash\)n");
13    \}
14    bdestroy(name);
15    bdestroy(descriptor);
16 \}
\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
The image metadata is attached to the Group within which all the Datasets are stored. The image metadata items are\+: {\ttfamily grouptype} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+Image\char`\"{}}), {\ttfamily descriptor}, {\ttfamily creation\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily history}, and {\ttfamily writeable}.

Note that until the image metadata is set up correctly the image is not recognized as a valid Geo\+Sci Image object, and so most functions in this library will not operate on it successfully. Because of this, the image creation functions, such as \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a6aebc2231c887d1bec1f10e361e649d9}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Create}, call this function as part of the creation process. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Delete@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Delete}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

16    return;

19           ...
\end{DoxyCode}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Get\+G\+S\+Children}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Get\+G\+S\+Children (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{object\+\_\+id, }

\item[{{\bf bstring} $\ast$$\ast$}]{objnames, }

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a19e538d571889073e925419460f8773a}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Get\+G\+S\+Children returns list of Geo\+Sci children objects. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & handle of an open object. The names of the children of this object, if any, are returned. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em nobjs} & The number of objects (children) found. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em objnames} & The returned list of object names. when done, bdestroy() each element, and G\+Free the container. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em objtypes} & The returned list of object types.~\newline
 G\+Free it when done.~\newline
 Valid values are\+:~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P 1~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+I\+M\+A\+G\+E 2~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R 3~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R2\+D 4~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R3\+D 5~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+N 6~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H2\+D 7~\newline
 G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+S\+H3\+D 8~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The routine returns T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Obtain list of objects in a file named \char`\"{}testimage.\+hd5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1     ...
2 bstring *objnames;
3 int objtypes;
4 int nobjs;
5 int i;
6 
7 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(bsstatic("testimage.hd5"),bsstatic("r+"));
8 if(file\_id<0)\{
9    printf("GS\_FileOpen failed\(\backslash\)n");
10    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
11    exit(-1);
12 \}//endif
13 
14 if(!GS\_ObjectGetGSChildren(file\_id, &nobjs, &objnames,&objtypes))\{
15    printf("GS\_ObjectGetGSChildren failed\(\backslash\)n");
16    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(error\_string));
17    exit(-1);
18 \}
19 
20 // print results:
21 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
22    printf("obj# %d: %s (%s)\(\backslash\)n",i,bdata(objnames[i]),
23            bdata(GS\_GSObjectTypeAsString(objtypes[i])) );
24 \}
25 
26 // clean up:
27 for(i=0;i<nobjs;i++)\{
28    bdestroy(objnames[i]);
29 \}
30 GFree(objnames);
31 GFree(objtypes);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

14    exit(-1);
15 \}//endif
16

19    printf("%s\(\backslash\)n",error\_string);
20    exit(-1);
21 \}
22 
23 // print results:

25    printf("obj# %d: %s (%s)\(\backslash\)n",i,objnames[i],
26            GS\_H5ObjectTypeAsString(objhdftypes[i]));
27 \}

Query about a raster named \char`\"{}r1\char`\"{} in an image named \char`\"{}\+Channel\+\_\+1\char`\"{}, in a file named \char`\"{}test123.\+h5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t    file\_id, image\_id;
2 bstring filename = bfromcstr("test123.h5");
3 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
4 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(filename,access);
5 if(file\_id < 0) \{
6    printf("Could not open file.\(\backslash\)n");
7    bdestroy(filename);
8    bdestroy(access);
9    return;
10 \}
11 bdestroy(filename);
12 bdestroy(access);
13 bstring channel=bfromcstr("Channel\_1");
14 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,channel);
15 if(image\_id < 0) \{
16    printf("Could not open image.\(\backslash\)n");
17    bdestroy(channel);
18    return;
19 \}
20 bdestroy(channel);
21 bstring dataset\_name = bfromcstr("r1");
22 if(GS\_ObjectIsDataset(image\_id,dataset\_name))\{
23    ... open the object as a dataset and do stuff ....
24 \} else \{
25    printf("Object is not a dataset.\(\backslash\)n");
26 \} // endif
27 bdestroy(dataset\_name);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E is returned if the object is a file, F\+A\+L\+S\+E otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}

4 C       \} else \{
5 C          printf("Object is not a file.\(\backslash\)n");
6 C       \} // endif
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

16 \} // endif

G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File determines if the object refers to a metadata internal-\/file. 

\label{hdf5mine_8h_GS_ObjectIsMetadataIFile}%
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_ObjectIsMetadataIFile}{}%
\index{GS_ObjectIsMetadataIFile@{GS\+\_\+ObjectIsMetadataIFile}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a73c5e5e7a3f2ae9e16abc78f0745e9f7}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D()}, \hyperlink{ifile_8h_a659760c048381d534347487e14cd5e25}{I\+File\+Open()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a1e9f0a9400fffd99b282b1dd651fa63d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Close()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & The handle of the open group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The name of the object within the group.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Open the Location metadata for an image and query if it\textquotesingle{}s valid Metadata I\+File\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 hid\_t group\_id;
3 bstring name = bfromcstr("/somename");
4 group\_id = GS\_GroupOpen(file\_id,name);
5 if(group\_id < 0) \{
6    printf("GS\_GroupOpen failed on /somename\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
8 bdestroy(name);
9 bstring location = bfromcstr("location");
10 if(!GS\_ObjectIsMetadataIFile(group\_id, location))\{
11   printf("Object is not a Metadata IFile.\(\backslash\)n");
12 \}
13 bdestroy(location);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
Some Metadata is stored as metadata items assocated with Groups, and other metadata is large enough that we create internal files (I\+Files) to store the data in. These files are like ordinary files, except that they are internal to the Geo\+Sci file. They can be binary, or text, and the arrangement of the data within them is specific to the Metadata that needs to be stored. The names of these I\+Files are used to determine the format. We have coders and ecoders for each format so that the actual format used does not need to be known by users of the system. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a73c5e5e7a3f2ae9e16abc78f0745e9f7}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Metadata\+I\+File\+By\+I\+D (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{dataset\+\_\+id}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a73c5e5e7a3f2ae9e16abc78f0745e9f7}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.

Open the Location metadata for an image and query if it\textquotesingle{}s valid Metadata I\+File\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 hid\_t objid;
3 bstring name = bfromcstr("someimage/location");
4 objid = GS\_DatasetOpen(file\_id,name);
5 if(objid < 0) \{
6    printf("GS\_DatasetOpen failed on /someimage/location\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
8 bdestroy(name);
9 if(!GS\_ObjectIsMetadataIFileByID(objid))\{
10   printf("Object is not a metadata internal file.\(\backslash\)n");
11 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
Some Metadata is stored as metadata items assocated with Groups, and other metadata is large enough that we create internal files (I\+Files) to store the data in. These files are like ordinary files, except that they are {\itshape internal} to the Geo\+Sci file. They can be binary, or text, and the arrangement of the data within them is specific to the Metadata that needs to be stored. The names of these I\+Files are used to determine the format. We have coders and ecoders for each format so that the actual format used does not need to be known by users of the system. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a1ffeb9b96d650a08d21867defe13c9fe}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Raster@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Raster}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Raster@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Is\+Raster}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a1ffeb9b96d650a08d21867defe13c9fe}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Lock makes an object read-\/only. 

\label{hdf5mine_8h_GS_ObjectLock}%
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_ObjectLock}{}%
\index{GS_ObjectLock@{GS\+\_\+ObjectLock}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a61d32b1e9d78286b2da48a300ce44ab2}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Object\+Unlock()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em id} & The handle of the file, or any object in the file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns T\+R\+U\+E if the object is now (or was already) read-\/only. Returns F\+A\+L\+S\+E if the object is still read/write, or on any error.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Make an image named \char`\"{}testimage\char`\"{} be read-\/only. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t object\_id;
2 bstring name = bfromcstr("testimage");
3 object\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,name);
4 if(object\_id < 0)\{
5   printf("Could not open the image.\(\backslash\)n");
6   return;
7 \}
8 bdestroy(name);
9 if(!GS\_ObjectLock(object\_id))\{
10   printf("Could not make image read-only.\(\backslash\)n");
11   return;
12 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
Yet\+: fill in details of how different object-\/types are handled. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+Dir returns the directory name of the pathname. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_abe4277ed46863da90a4fdf7ee2ec35b9}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The pathname to process.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a bstring of the stripped name, which has zero length if there is any kind of error. bdestroy() it when done.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
This example starts with a path of \char`\"{}/some/path/name/here/blah\char`\"{} and the returned value from G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+Dir is\+: \char`\"{}/some/path/name/here\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring longname=bfromcstr("/some/path/name/here/blah");
2 bstring the\_name;
3 the\_name = GS\_PathnameGetDir(longname);
4 if(bstrlen(the\_name)==0)\{
5   printf("Could not determine the name\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
7 printf("The directory name is: %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(the\_name));
8 bdestroy(the\_name);
9 bdestroy(long\_name);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
For filenames that have no \char`\"{}/\char`\"{} characters (\textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{} in windows), a zero-\/length string is returned. It\textquotesingle{}s not null. It still needs to be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when you are done with it. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a5164d33a06aceae6514d233d1570bc9e}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+H\+D\+F\+Dir@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+H\+D\+F\+Dir}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+No\+Dir(), \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_abe4277ed46863da90a4fdf7ee2ec35b9}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join()}

Assumes directories are separated with \char`\"{}/\char`\"{}. For filenames that have no \char`\"{}/\char`\"{} characters, a zero-\/length string is returned. It\textquotesingle{}s not null. It still needs to be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when you are done with it. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_abe4277ed46863da90a4fdf7ee2ec35b9}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join}}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf bstring} G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{front, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{back}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_abe4277ed46863da90a4fdf7ee2ec35b9}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join joins 2 pieces of a pathname. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a6d72093c09d6975d8e2d93d54a714731}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+Dir()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em front} & The front part of the pathname. Should not end with a \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} or a \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em back} & The back part of the pathname. Should not start or end end with a \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} or a \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a bstring of the joined names, which has zero length if there is any kind of error. bdestroy() it when done.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
This example starts with a path of \char`\"{}/some/path/name/here/blah\char`\"{} and a relative filename of \char`\"{}trash.\+dat\char`\"{}. The returned value from G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join (on unix) is\+: \char`\"{}/some/path/name/here/blah/trash.\+dat\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring longname=bfromcstr("/some/path/name/here/blah");
2 bstring ending=bfromcstr("trash.dat");
3 bstring the\_name;
4 the\_name = GS\_PathnameJoin(longname,ending);
5 if(bstrlen(the\_name)==0)\{
6   printf("Could not join the names\(\backslash\)n");
7   return;
8 \}
9 printf("The joined name is: %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(the\_name));
10 bdestroy(the\_name);
11 bdestroy(longname);
12 bdestroy(ending);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
It uses the correct joining character for the operating system\+: for L\+I\+N\+U\+X, M\+A\+C\+O\+S\+: \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}, for Windows\+: \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{}. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_af2e3e58534e4bb18cdcf1a62a3829914}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Nodir@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Nodir}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Nodir@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Nodir}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{name}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_af2e3e58534e4bb18cdcf1a62a3829914}

\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a6d72093c09d6975d8e2d93d54a714731}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Get\+Dir()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_abe4277ed46863da90a4fdf7ee2ec35b9}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+Join()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The pathname to process.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a bstring of the stripped name, which has zero length if there is any kind of error. bdestroy() it when done.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
This example starts with a path of \char`\"{}/some/path/name/here/blah\char`\"{} and the returned value from G\+S\+\_\+\+Pathname\+No\+Dir is\+: \char`\"{}blah\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring longname=bfromcstr("/some/path/name/here/blah");
2 bstring the\_name;
3 the\_name = GS\_PathnameNoDir(longname);
4 if(bstrlen(the\_name)==0)\{
5   printf("Could not determine the name\(\backslash\)n");
6 \}
7 printf("The stripped name is: %s\(\backslash\)n",bdata(the\_name));
8 bdestroy(the\_name);
9 bdestroy(long\_name);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
For filenames that end with a \char`\"{}/\char`\"{} (\textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{} in windows), a zero-\/length string is returned. It\textquotesingle{}s not null. It still needs to be bdestroy()\textquotesingle{}d when you are done with it. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{image\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{raster\+\_\+name, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{window}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aad432d0513d576bfa0204514a58da96d}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window checks whether a requested window selection is within the bounds of an image. It will also default a window specification to be the whole image if X\+Size and/or Y\+Size are zero. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a92c52acc14a0fd4566b4c2c50f33322a}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window\+By\+I\+D()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+id} & Image handle that has the raster in it. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+name} & Name of raster to check. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em window} & Vector containing desired window specification\+:~\newline
window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} = Xoffset~\newline
window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} = Yoffset~\newline
window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} = Xsize~\newline
window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} = Ysize~\newline
~\newline
If window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is 0, window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} will be set to image X size -\/ window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}. ~\newline
If window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} is 0, window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} will be set to image Y size -\/ window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E is returned on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
In this example a Geo\+Sci raster is opened and a user specified window is checked for validity in one of its images. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1               ...
2 hid\_t      image\_id;
3 int        window[4];
4               ...
5 window[0]=0;
6 window[1]=0;
7 window[2]=512;
8 window[3]=1024;
9 if(!GS\_RasterCheckWindow( image\_id, bsstatic("r1"), window)) \{
10      printf("GS\_RasterCheckWindow failure.\(\backslash\)n");
11 \}
12              ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window\+By\+I\+D checks whether a requested window selection is within the bounds of a raster. It will also default a window specification to be the whole raster if X\+Size and/or Y\+Size are zero. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_aad432d0513d576bfa0204514a58da96d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Check\+Window} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} = Xoffset~\newline
window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} = Yoffset~\newline
window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} = Xsize~\newline
window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} = Ysize~\newline
~\newline
If window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is 0, on return window\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} will be set to image X size -\/ window\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}. ~\newline
If window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} is 0, on return window\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} will be set to image Y size -\/ window\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

T\+R\+U\+E is returned on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
In this example a Geo\+Sci file and raster is opened and a user specified window is checked for validity in one of its rasters. 
\begin{DoxyCode}

3 int        window[4];
4               ...
5 bstring file = bfromcstr("blah.h5");

7 if(!file\_id) \{
8    printf("GS\_FileOpen failed.\(\backslash\)n");
9    exit(-1);
10 \}
11 
12 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen( file\_id, "/image1" );
13 if(!image\_id) \{
14    printf("GS\_ImageOpen failed.\(\backslash\)n");
15    exit(-1);
16 \}
17 
18 raster\_id = GS\_RasterOpen( file\_id, "r5" );
19 if(!raster\_id) \{
20    printf("GS\_RasterOpen failed.\(\backslash\)n");
21    exit(-1);
22 \}
23 
24 window[0]=0;
25 window[1]=0;
26 window[2]=512;
27 window[3]=1024;
28 if(!GS\_RasterCheckWindowByID( raster\_id, window)) \{
29      printf("GS\_RasterCheckWindowByID failure.\(\backslash\)n");
30 \}
31              ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create create new image raster for a Geo\+Sci Image. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab4ba5f75f8d6bf779f23430b76da74fc}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Open}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a97858319e71528313dd92f9ad9c57ea3}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Close}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a8483fc8490257c640e33fc5319fda77a}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Delete}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+name} & The name of the raster channel to create. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+type} & The type for the raster data. One of\+:~\newline
 D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1 1 A single bit~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer~\newline

 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 16 Signed 64-\/bit integer~\newline
\\
\hline

\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em nlines} & The y-\/dimension of the raster channel. \\

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The handle for the created raster is returned. This handle is less than zero if there is any error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Create the raster named \char`\"{}r7\char`\"{} for an image named \char`\"{}/image3\char`\"{} in an already-\/open Geo\+Sci file. The raster should be a 32-\/bit-\/real image, with 1024 pixels X 512 lines. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id, image\_id, raster\_id;
2 bstring image\_name = bfromcstr("/image3");
3 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,image\_name);
4 bdestroy(image\_name);
5 if(image\_id < 0 )\{
6   printf("GS\_ImageOpen failure\(\backslash\)n");
7   exit(-1);
8 \}
9 bstring descriptor = bfromcstr("Howland-IR");
10 bstring name = bfromcstr("r7");
11 raster\_id = GS\_RasterCreate(image\_id,name,GS\_DATATYPE\_R32,1024,512,descriptor);
12 bdestroy(descriptor);
13 bdestroy(name);
14 if(raster\_id<0)\{
15   printf("GS\_RasterCreate failure\(\backslash\)n");
16   exit(-1);
17 \}
18 
19 .... do stuff ....
20 
21 GS\_RasterClose(raster\_id);
22 GS\_ImageClose(image\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This function defaults the pixel size metadata\+: {\ttfamily pixel\+\_\+size\+\_\+\+\_\+units=\char`\"{}meter\char`\"{}}, {\ttfamily pixels\+\_\+size\+\_\+x=1.\+0}, {\ttfamily pixel\+\_\+size\+\_\+y=1.\+0}. These can be reset to valid values using the function G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create\+Metadata fills the standard raster metadata attributes with the values that are passed in. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Image\+Add()
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+id} & The I\+D of the image that contains this raster. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+name} & A character string giving the name of the existing raster in the image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+type} & The type for the raster data. One of\+:~\newline
 D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1 1 A single bit~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} 4 Complex 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} 5 Unsigned 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 16 Signed 64-\/bit integer~\newline
\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em npixels} & The x-\/dimension of the raster channel. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em nlines} & The y-\/dimension of the raster channel. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em descriptor} & A character string describing the image contents.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
After creating a new raster named \char`\"{}r3\char`\"{} in an image named \char`\"{}datatake 34\char`\"{} in a file named \char`\"{}av1.\+h5\char`\"{}, we must set the metadata for the raster before the raster object can be used. The descriptor is \char`\"{}\+S\+I\+R\+C-\/\+S\+L\+C data from S\+R\+L-\/1 over Greenland\char`\"{}. The raster datatype is complex-\/integer, each 32 bits, with 1024 pixels along the x-\/direction, and 2048 lines along the y-\/dimension.


\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 hid\_t image\_id;
3 bstring filename=bfromcstr("av1.h5");
4 bstring access=bfromcstr("r+");
5 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(filename,access);
6 bdestroy(filename);
7 bdestroy(access);
8 
9 if(file\_id > 0) \{
10    bstring image\_name =bfromcstr("datatake 34");
11    bstring image\_descriptor = bfromcstr("sirc data");
12    image\_id = GS\_ImageCreate(file\_id,image\_name,image\_descriptor);
13    bdestroy(image\_name);
14    bdestroy(image\_descriptor);
15    
16    if(image\_id>0)\{
17       ... create a new dataset that represents the Raster...
18 
19       bstring name = bfromcstr("r3");
20       bstring descriptor = bfromcstr("SIRC-SLC data from SRL-1 over Greenland");
21       if(GS\_RasterCreateMetadata(image\_id,raster\_name,GS\_DATATYPE\_CI32,
22                                  1024,2048,descriptor)\{
23          printf("success\(\backslash\)n");
24       \}
25       bdestroy(name);
26       bdestroy(descriptor);
27    \}
28    GS\_ImageClose(image\_id);
29 \}
30 GS\_FileClose(file\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
The raster metadata is attached to the Dataset that holds the raster data. The raster metadata items are\+: ~\newline
{\ttfamily dataset\+\_\+type} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+Raster\char`\"{}}),~\newline
{\ttfamily pixel\+\_\+size\+\_\+units} (default is {\ttfamily \char`\"{}meter\char`\"{}}), ~\newline
{\ttfamily pixel\+\_\+size\+\_\+x},~\newline
{\ttfamily pixel\+\_\+size\+\_\+y},~\newline
{\ttfamily type}, ~\newline
{\ttfamily npixels}, ~\newline
{\ttfamily nlines}, ~\newline
{\ttfamily descriptor},~\newline
{\ttfamily creation\+\_\+datetime},~\newline
 {\ttfamily last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime},~\newline
 {\ttfamily history}, ~\newline
 and {\ttfamily writeable}.

Note that until the raster metadata is set up correctly the raster is not recognized as a valid Geo\+Sci Raster object, and so most functions in this library will not operate on it successfully. Because of this, the raster creation functions, such as \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a895023bd9cb5070686c7bcd0159e2133}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create}, call this function as part of the creation process. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Delete deletes an existing raster. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a461ac5bcc8e05be64b6b23e75872f968}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Image\+Open}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab4ba5f75f8d6bf779f23430b76da74fc}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Open}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a97858319e71528313dd92f9ad9c57ea3}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Close} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+id} & Handle of containing image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+name} & Name of raster to delete. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Delete a raster named \char`\"{}r3\char`\"{} in image named \char`\"{}/\+Channel\+\_\+1\char`\"{} in a file named \char`\"{}test123.\+h5\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1            ...
2 hid\_t    file\_id;
3 bstring name = bfromcstr("test123.h5");
4 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
5 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(name,access);
6 bdestroy(name);
7 bdstroy(access);
8 if(file\_id < 0) \{
9    printf("Could not open file.\(\backslash\)n");
10    return;
11 \}
12 
13 bstring image\_name = bfromcstr("/Channel\_1");
14 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,image\_name);
15 bdestroy(image\_name);
16 if(image\_id < 0) \{
17    printf("Could not open image.\(\backslash\)n");
18    return;
19 \}
20 
21 bstring raster\_name = bfromcstr("r3");
22 if(!GS\_RasterDelete(image\_id,raster\_name))\{
23    printf("raster deletion failed.\(\backslash\)n");
24    bdestroy(raster\_name);
25    return;
26 \}
27 bdestroy(raster\_name);
28           ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ab4ba5f75f8d6bf779f23430b76da74fc}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Open@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Open}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Open opens existing raster dataset. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ab917a3df2cea2e72a959d8e72d8b7f5d}{G\+S\+\_\+\+File\+Open}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a895023bd9cb5070686c7bcd0159e2133}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a97858319e71528313dd92f9ad9c57ea3}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Close} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em image\+\_\+id} & Image handle in a G\+E\+O\+S\+C\+I file \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+name} & Name of raster dataset to open. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A handle to the raster dataset is returned on success, while a value less than 0 is returned on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Open an image named \char`\"{}\+Channel\+\_\+1\char`\"{} in a file named \char`\"{}test123.\+h5\char`\"{}, and then open the raster, which is named \char`\"{}r1\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1            ...
2 hid\_t    file\_id, image\_id, raster\_id;
3 bstring name = bfromcstr("test123.h5");
4 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
5 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(name, access);
6 bdestroy(access);
7 bdestroy(name);
8 if(file\_id < 0) \{
9    printf("Could not open file.\(\backslash\)n");
10    return;
11 \}
12 
13 bstring image\_name = bfromcstr("/Channel\_1");
14 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,image\_name);
15 bdestroy(image\_name);
16 if(image\_id < 0) \{
17    printf("Could not open image.\(\backslash\)n");
18    return;
19 \}
20 
21 bstring raster\_name = bfromcstr("r1");
22 raster\_id = GS\_RasterOpen(image\_id,raster\_name);
23 bdestroy(raster\_name);
24 if(raster\_id < 0) \{
25    printf("Could not open raster.\(\backslash\)n");
26    return;
27 \}
28           ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a66829cf51f9c3d01819df25398b23620}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{raster\+\_\+id, }
\item[{int}]{func, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{x\+\_\+pixelsize, }
\item[{double $\ast$}]{y\+\_\+pixelsize, }
\item[{{\bf bstring}}]{pixel\+\_\+units}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_a66829cf51f9c3d01819df25398b23620}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size reads/writes Raster Pixel Size. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a895023bd9cb5070686c7bcd0159e2133}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Create} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+id} & Handle to already-\/opened Raster in a Geo\+Sci file. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em func} & Flag indicating whether to write the passed pixel size to the image metadata (G\+S\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+E), or return the pixel size currently stored for the image (G\+S\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+D). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em x\+\_\+pixelsize} & Pixel ground X-\/size in `pixel\+\_\+units\textquotesingle{} units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em y\+\_\+pixelsize} & Pixel ground Y-\/size in `pixel\+\_\+units\textquotesingle{} units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em pixel\+\_\+units} & Pixel Size Units string. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned on success, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
The following code prints out the current pixel size information, and then sets the pixel size to 1 meter by 1 meter. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t      raster\_id;
2 double     xsize, ysize;
3 bstring    pixel\_units=bfromcstr("");
4 ...
5 if(GS\_RasterPixelSize( raster\_id, GS\_READ, &xsize, &ysize, pixel\_units ))\{
6    printf( "Pixel Size was %g x %g %s\(\backslash\)n", 
7          xsize, ysize, bdata(pixel\_units) );
8 \}
9 
10 xsize = 1.0;
11 ysize = 1.0;
12 bassigncstr(pixel\_units,"meter");
13 if(GS\_RasterPixelSize( raster\_id, GS\_WRITE, &xsize, &ysize, pixel\_units ))\{
14    printf( "Pixel size reset to 1 x 1 Meters.\(\backslash\)n" );
15 \}
16 bdestroy(pixel\_units);
17 ...
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details}
This is useful for rasters that have no projection, or whose projection and spatial system are only loosely known. In other cases, using the projection information and the coordinates information in other metadata collections is preferred. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ae7010dc876746d014471d099ba5c0518}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{raster\+\_\+id, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{npixels, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{nlines}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ae7010dc876746d014471d099ba5c0518}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Size\+Info returns the number of pixels and lines in a raster. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a66829cf51f9c3d01819df25398b23620}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Pixel\+Size()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em raster\+\_\+id} & Handle for opened raster in a Geosci file. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em npixels} & Pointer to integer to be loaded with the number of image pixels. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em nlines} & Pointer to integer to be loaded with the number of image lines. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
On success, T\+R\+U\+E is returned, otherwise F\+A\+L\+S\+E is returned, and -\/1 for the values of both npixels and nlines.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Provide the user with information about a previously opened raster. The program prints the number of pixels per line and lines per image. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t fileid, image\_id, raster\_id;
2 int npixels, nlines;
3 
4 // open the file:
5 bstring file\_name = bfromcstr("blah.h5");
6 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen( file\_name, bsstatic("r") ); 
7 if(file\_id < 0)\{
8    printf("Can't open the file  %s.\(\backslash\)n",bdata(file\_name));
9    return FALSE;
10 \}// endif
11 
12 // open the image
13 bstring image\_name = bfromcstr("/Image1");
14 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id, image\_name);
15 if(image\_id < 0)\{
16    printf("Can't open the image %s.\(\backslash\)n",bdata(image\_name));
17    return FALSE;
18 \}// endif
19 
20 //open the raster:
21 bstring raster\_name = bfromcstr("raster4");
22 raster\_id = GS\_RasterOpen(image\_id,raster\_name);
23 if(raster\_id < 0)\{
24    printf("Can't open the raster %s.\(\backslash\)n",bdata(raster\_name));
25    return FALSE;
26 \}// endif
27 
28 if(GS\_RasterSizeInfo( raster\_id, &npixels, &nlines ))\{
29    printf( " Pixels: %d\(\backslash\)n Lines: %d\(\backslash\)n",
30            npixels, nlines );
31 \} else \{
32    printf("Can't get Raster size information.\(\backslash\)n");
33 \}
34 GS\_RasterClose(raster\_id);
35 GS\_ImageClose(image\_id);
36 GS\_FileClose(file\_id);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a8ee578c235946d66f642cbe73994b0d3}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Type\+Is\+Complex@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Raster\+Type\+Is\+Complex}}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & An integer representing a Geo\+Sci datatype. Valid datatypes\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I1} 1 A single bit~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I8} 2 Unsigned 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I8} 3 Signed 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I8} 4 Complex 8-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I16} 5 Unsigned 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I16} 6 Signed 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I16} 7 Complex 16-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I32} 8 Unsigned 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I32} 9 Signed 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32} 10 Complex 32-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I64} 11 Complex 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R32} 12 32-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+R64} 13 64-\/bit Real number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C64} 14 Complex 64-\/bit floating-\/point number~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C128} 15 Complex 128-\/bit floating point ~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+U\+I64} 16 Unsigned 64-\/bit integer~\newline
 {\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+S\+I64} 17 Signed 64-\/bit integer~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned for complex types, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} for scalar types and {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+O\+R} otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Query if the type G\+S\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+I32 is a complex type\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 int result;
2 result = GS\_RasterTypeIsComplex(GS\_DATATYPE\_CI32);
3 if( result == TRUE ) \{
4    printf("It's a complex type\(\backslash\)n");
5 \} else if( result == FALSE )\{
6    printf("It's a scalar type\(\backslash\)n");
7 \} else \{
8    printf("Error!\(\backslash\)n");
9 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Set\+Cache\+Size sets the metadata cache size for a Geo\+Sci datafile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & File handle for Geo\+Sci datafile \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em cache\+\_\+size} & Size in bytes for the metadata cache. 1048576 (1 M\+Byte) is a good default.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A non-\/negative integer is returned on success, while a negative integer is returned on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}
Set the cache size to be 1\+M\+Byte\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}

3    printf("Error setting cache size.\(\backslash\)n");
4 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em group\+\_\+id} & The opened object where the attribute is stored.\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The name of the attribute variable.\\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & The value of the variable to set.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Set the group type attribute\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring group\_type=bfromcstr("");
2 hid\_t object\_id;
3 bassigncstr(group\_type,"unknown type");
4 if(!GS\_SetStringAttribute(object\_id,bsstatic("grouptype"),group\_type))\{
5    printf("Unable to set group-type string\(\backslash\)n");
6 \} else \{
7    printf("Group-type successfully set.\(\backslash\)n");
8 \}// endif
9 ... use group\_type ...
10 bdestroy(group\_type);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_ac06fa696ae73810823550a574fc9ffbc}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{history\+\_\+string, }
\item[{{\bf bstring}}]{front, }
\item[{{\bf bstring}}]{back}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_ac06fa696ae73810823550a574fc9ffbc}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Split\+History splits history string into front and back. 

\label{hdf5mine_8h_GS_SplitHistory}%
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_SplitHistory}{}%
\index{GS_SplitHistory@{GS\+\_\+SplitHistory}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a7b6825b73fd902fa82581428da61334e}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+History()}, \hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_a66495bd84e6c728dd308b75db7f32cbf}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Aborted\+History()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{\mbox{[}in\mbox{]} history\+\_\+string}
The input history string. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{\mbox{[}out\mbox{]} front}
The output front of the history string, with the last line, if any, stripped off. On input, this must be a valid bstring. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{\mbox{[}out\mbox{]} back}
The output back of the history string, containing the last line, if any. On input, this must be a valid bstring.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Given a history string like\+: ~\newline
 {\ttfamily \char`\"{}line1;\textbackslash{}nline2;\textbackslash{}nline3;\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{}} ~\newline
 This function returns\+: ~\newline
front = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\textbackslash{}line1;\textbackslash{}nline2;\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{}} back = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}line3;\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{}}  This is programmed as\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring history=bfromcstr("line1;\(\backslash\)nline2;\(\backslash\)nline3;\(\backslash\)n");
2 bstring front  =bfromcstr("");
3 bstring back   =bfromcstr("");
4 
5 GS\_SplitHistory(history,front, back);
6 
7      ... use front and back ...
8 
9 bdestroy(history);
10 bdestroy(front);
11 bdestroy(back);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
The history string is made up of lines delimited by \char`\"{};\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{}. There are several cases\+:

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the history string is empty, then 2 empty strings are returned.\end{DoxyItemize}
li If the history string is non-\/empty, but has no \char`\"{};\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{} delimiters, then the returned front string is empty, and the back string is this string, with a \char`\"{};\textbackslash{}n\char`\"{} appended to it.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the history string has 1 line, then the returned front string is empty, and the back string is this 1 line.\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In all other cases, all but the the last line is copied to the front string, and the last line is copied into the back string. \end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_aaf97760ec3c800c9e77adae19c54efc0}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aaf97760ec3c800c9e77adae19c54efc0}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Update\+Metadata update a metadata item for the given object. 

\label{hdf5mine_8h_GS_UpdateMetadata}%
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_UpdateMetadata}{}%
\index{GS_UpdateMetadata@{GS\+\_\+UpdateMetadata}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{hdf5mine_8h_ae74518625827cc1a4edc417eb54a59ca}{G\+S\+\_\+\+Append\+Metadata}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+id} & I\+D of Geo\+Sci object to modify. Can be a file, an image, etc. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The name of the metadata variable to modify. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em value} & The new value for the metadata variable.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Change the {\ttfamily descriptor} metadata for an image to \char`\"{}\+Angkor Wat, Cambodia\char`\"{}. 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t image\_id;
2 bstring name = bfromcstr("/image45");
3 image\_id = GS\_ImageOpen(file\_id,name);
4 bdestroy(name);
5 if(!image\_id) \{
6   printf("Failed to open the image\(\backslash\)n");
7 \}
8 bstring descriptor = bfromcstr("descriptor");
9 bstring descriptor\_value = bfromcstr("Angkor Wat, Cambodia");
10 if(!GS\_UpdateMetadata(image\_id,descriptor,descriptor\_value)))\{
11   printf("Failed to modify image descriptor\(\backslash\)n");
12 \}
13 bdestroy(descriptor);
14 bdestroy(descriptor\_value);
\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a1bde4d83ab42554ee87e41fec520013a}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Valid\+I\+D@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Valid\+I\+D}}

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_a7e1ab917fd45b92dfe8e35f8b1bf0912}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Valid\+Metadata\+Name@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Valid\+Metadata\+Name}}

G\+S\+\_\+\+Valid\+Metadata\+Name check if the name is a valid metadata item for the given object type.

\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_GS_ValidMetadataName}{}%

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em object\+\_\+type} & An integer giving the type of object this metadata variable refers to. Valid object types are\+: ~\newline

{\ttfamily G\+S\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+I\+F\+I\+L\+E} 13 \\

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\ttfamily T\+R\+U\+E} is returned if the name is a valid metadata variable, {\ttfamily F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}
Make sure that {\ttfamily descriptor} is a valid metadata item for an image before updating its value\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
1 bstring name = bfromcstr("descriptor");
2 if(!GS\_ValidMetadataName(GS\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_IMAGE, name))\{
3    printf("not a valid image metadata variable.\(\backslash\)n");
4 \}
5 bdestroy(name);
\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
Because the metadata updating functions will not only update, but also create new metadata items, this function is used to prevent mis-\/spellings of valid metadata items, and also to prevent accidental creation of new metadata items. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\hypertarget{hdf5mine_8h_aca52414a3f6f3da1cfc4b4dcdbfc5a9c}{}\index{hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}!G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata}}
\index{G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata@{G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata}!hdf5mine.\+h@{hdf5mine.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{hid\+\_\+t}]{file\+\_\+id, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{vector\+\_\+name, }
\item[{{\bf const\+\_\+bstring}}]{descriptor}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{hdf5mine_8h_aca52414a3f6f3da1cfc4b4dcdbfc5a9c}


G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create\+Metadata creates vector metadata. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create()
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em file\+\_\+id} & The file I\+D. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em vector\+\_\+name} & A character string giving the name of the image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em descriptor} & A character string describing the vector contents.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
T\+R\+U\+E on success, F\+A\+L\+S\+E on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example\+:}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
After creating a new vector named \char`\"{}hydrology\char`\"{} in a file named \char`\"{}av1.\+h5\char`\"{}, we must set the metadata for the vector object before it can be used. The descriptor is \char`\"{}water boundaries\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyCode}
1 hid\_t file\_id;
2 bstring name = bfromcstr("av1.h5");
3 bstring access = bfromcstr("r+");
4 file\_id = GS\_FileOpen(name,access);
5 bdestroy(name);
6 bdestroy(access);
7 if(file\_id > 0) \{
8    ... create a group with a dataset in it that represent the vector information...
9    bstring vname = bfromcstr("hydrology");
10    bstring vdescriptor = bfromcstr("water boundaries");
11    if(GS\_VectorCreateMetadata(file\_id,vname,vdescriptor)\{
12       printf("success\(\backslash\)n");
13    \}
14    bdestroy(vname);
15    bdestroy(vdescriptor);
16 \}
\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Details\+:}
The vector metadata is attached to the Group within which the vector Dataset is stored. The vector metadata items are\+: {\ttfamily grouptype} (= {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\+Image\char`\"{}}), {\ttfamily descriptor}, {\ttfamily creation\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily last\+\_\+update\+\_\+datetime}, {\ttfamily history}, {\ttfamily writeable} and {\ttfamily spatialref}.

Note that until the vector metadata is set up correctly the image is not recognized as a valid Geo\+Sci Vector object, and so most functions in this library will not operate on it successfully. Because of this, the vector creation function, G\+S\+\_\+\+Vector\+Create calls this function as part of the creation process. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}
